כותרת: The effects of generative AI usage on employee knowledge behavior: a perspective based on the Automation–Augmentation Paradox
קישור: https://www.frontiersin.org/journals/psychology/articles/10.3389/fpsyg.2026.1847724/full
תאריך: 2026-06-26
קטגוריה: Hybrid Intelligence
